W1PD107937:::de yang mnga' ris paN chen chos kyi rgyal po'i gsung las/ /rnying ma tshad ldan zhig byed na bka' mas khog phug gter ma'i man ngag gis brgyan pa zhig dgos zhes gsung ba dang / rdo rje 'chang pha bong kha pas kyang bla ma dam pa bsod nams rgyal mtshan gyi mdzad pa'i phur pa 'di la/ sbyang gzhi sbyong byed sogs lam gyi 'gros rnams snga 'gyur gyi gsung rab gong ma rnams kyi dgongs pa'i gnad tshang zhing / gsar ma'i rgyal bkab ma yin pa'i rnying nyams chen po zhig yang gsung pa yang yang thogs shing / bka' ma'i rgyud dang sgrub thabs rnams la bltas kyang de kho na ltar snang la/ gter kha gong 'og gnyis kyang bka' ma dang mthun chas che ba mang / grub thob me long rdo rje'i chos sgrigs der mkhas pa mang pos legs so mdzad mod/ o rgyan chen pos dus gsum bsgribs med du gzigs pas gdul bya'i blo mchog dman bar gsum dang bstun pa'i gter kha so sor dus skabs dang bstun pa'i rgyas bsdus sna tshogs yong bar gor ma chag rung / deng sang rnying rlom rgyal khams ma mthong a ma'i gsang gnas la mtshar 'dzin du mas gter gzhung tshig nyung tsho dang mthun na rnying ma yin la/ de min gsar ma nas lhad bcug go snyam pa'i log rtog (21na) dang bgros gleng ba mang mod/ lha sras rnam sprul bar gsan ma thub pas gter chen chos kyi rgyal po legs ldan rdo rje'i drung du rdzogs par gsan cing / dpon slob gnyis bka' bgros pa'i thog nas bskyed rdzogs 'bring po'i thog nas bskyed rdzogs 'bring grol drung du gter kha gong 'og byang gter gyi bka' brgyad gsum tshang ba dang / khyab bdag khra (21ba) tshang ba chen por gsang rdzogs bskyar ba ldabs shin tu rgyas pa/ chos rgyal gter bdag gling par W294:::ces rigs gsum 'dus pa 'jam dpal khro chu dug sdong nag po'i bsnyen pa'i yi ge rin cen ke ta ka 'di ni snga 'gyur bstan pa'i nyi ma chen po rig 'dzin sprul pa'i sku blo bzang pad+ma 'phrin las rnams sngags 'chang dkon cog lhun grub kyi rgyun las mkhas grub khra tshang pa chen por thos shing/ rat+na gnyis pa mtshungs med chos kyi grags pa'i thun mong ma yin pa'i gsung rgyun rnams ban grong sngags 'chang mchog gtub rgyal por phyag khrid zhun thar bcad pas gshin rje mkhan po'i gral du sdod pa la ma nongs pa'i za hor gyi sngags smyon zil gnon bzhad pa rtsal gyis me sbrul hor zla brgyad pa'i khrag 'thung rnam par rol pa'i tshes la rgyal khab dmar po rir sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni rig 'dzin gyi btsun pa 'jam dbyangs grags pas bgyis shing/ dus dbang gis gal chung chos la bye par ma zad gshed skor 'di nyid dkon zhing gdams pa rnams kha 'thor ba'i nyag phra bar snang bas zhal shes yig chung gis legs par brgyan nas gsal bar bkod pa brgyud pa'i khungs la mi sems shing/ rang gi gegs sel tsam du rma khar phan na khyi tshil du byed pa sogs snod min la gsang zhing sba ba'i bka' rgya yod pas 'chal bar spyod na 'chi bdag las kyi gshin rjes tshar chod cig gu hya sa mA yA// //sabra mang+ga laM/:::ces rigs gsum 'dus pa 'jam dpal khro chu dug sdong nag po'i bsnyen pa'i yi ge rin cen ke ta ka 'di ni snga 'gyur bstan pa'i nyi ma chen po rig 'dzin sprul pa'i sku blo bzang pad+ma 'phrin las W294:::ces gshin rje gza' gdong dmar nag gi lag len sgo 'byed kyi lde mig 'di ni rnam par rgyal ba'i phan bde legs bshad gling pa rnams kyi nyams len du byed 'dun yod pa'i steng nye char mchod dpon ngag dbang shes rab kyis mtshams sbyar ba la brten nas za hor gyi sngags nag zil gnon drag rtsal gyis chu glang hor zla lnga pa'i tshes bcu bzhi la pho brang po ta lar sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni sngags btsun 'jam dbyangs grags pas bgyis pa dam med snod min lag tu shor na stod yul dang ston mkhan gnyis ka chos skyong stag zhon nag po dang gter srung mthu chen sde bzhis tshar gcod pa'i 'phrin las mdzod cig gu hya sa ma ya/:::ces gshin rje gza' gdong dmar nag gi lag len sgo 'byed kyi lde mig 'di ni rnam par rgyal ba'i phan bde legs bshad gling pa rnams kyi nyams len du byed 'dun yod pa'i steng nye char mchod dpon ngag dbang shes rab kyis mtshams sbyar ba la brten nas za hor gyi sngags nag zil gnon drag rtsal gyis chu glang hor zla lnga pa'i tshes bcu bzhi la pho brang po ta lar sbyar ba'i yi ge pa ni sngags btsun 'jam dbyangs grags pas bgyis pa dam med snod min lag tu shor na stod yul dang ston mkhan gnyis ka chos skyong stag zhon nag po dang gter srung mthu chen sde bzhis tshar gcod pa'i 'phrin las mdzod cig gu h+ya sa ma ya/
W23918:::rje btsun rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub dkyil gyi cho ga'i ngag 'don 'di yang bstan 'dzin chos rje'i mtshan gyis byin gyis brlabs pas ye shes lhun grub kyis gzhung lugs gzhan gyi bsre bslad med par legs par bshad pa gu hya sa ma ya rgya/ khyad chos lnga ldan rdo rje'i rgyas btab pa'i/ /zab don rtogs dka' bdag blo mthu dman pas// nongs gyur mchis na bla ma mkha' 'gro yis/ /bzod par gsol la sdig ltung sbyang du gsol/ /'dir 'bad dge bas bdag dang 'gro ba kun/ /lhan skyes bde chen rdo rje rnal 'byor mar//rol pa'i rtse dgas 'tsho zhing lcags zam pa'i//bstan pa rin chen yun ring 'bar gyur cig/ dge'o//mang+ga laM//:::rje btsun rdo rje phag mo'i sgrub dkyil gyi cho ga'i ngag 'don 'di yang bstan 'dzin chos rje'i mtshan gyis byin gyis brlabs pas ye shes lhun grub kyis gzhung lugs gzhan gyi bsre bslad med par legs par bshad pa gu h+ya sa ma ya rgya/ kh+yad chos lnga ldan rdo rje'i rgyas btab pa'i/ /zab don rtogs dka' bdag blo mthu dman pas// nongs gyur mchis na bla ma mkha' 'gro yis/ /bzod par gsol la sdig ltung sbyang du gsol/ /'dir 'bad dge bas bdag dang 'gro ba kun/ /lhan skyes bde chen rdo rje rnal 'byor mar//rol pa'i rtse dgas 'tsho zhing lcags zam pa'i//bstan pa rin chen yun ring 'bar gyur cig/ dge'o//mang+ga laM//

W4CZ1042:::'di yang / lam 'dir mos pa mi phyed dge ba can rang slob rdo bla oDI ya na'i mtshan 'dzin nas/ sngar gyi dz+nyA shrI b+h dra'i chog khrigs zhib mor bzhugs kyang phal cher tshan thor du gyur pa dang 'ga' zhig rjes 'jug rnams kyis/ rang 'dod bzhin gsar btsud mdzad pas rtsa ba'i sa bcad 'khrugs shing lta mi bde bar gyur pa dang / gzhan yang du ma zlos skyon can sogs bdag 'dra'i blo dman
